Grafana unified alerting subsystem is implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/` and consists of several interconnected major components:\\n\\n## 1. Service Orchestrator (`ngalert.go`)\\n\\nThe main entry point is `AlertNG` in `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`. The `ProvideService()` function initializes all components and `AlertNG.Run()` orchestrates their execution. The architecture follows a typical pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Alert Rule Storage** receives rules from the database\\n2. **Scheduler** fetches rules and determines evaluation timing\\n3. **Evaluator** executes rule queries against data sources\\n4. **State Manager** tracks alert state transitions\\n5. **History Writer** persists state changes for audit/dashboards\\n6. **Notifier** sends alerts through Alertmanager\\n7. **Alerts Router** dispatches to external Alertmanagers\\n\\n## 2. Alert Rule Storage (`store/`)\\n\\nThe storage layer is implemented by `DBstore` in `pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go`. This component manages:\\n\\n- **Alert Rules**: `store/alert_rule.go` - CRUD operations for alert rules\\n- **Alertmanager Config**: `store/alertmanager.go` - Configuration storage and versioning\\n- **Alert Instances**: Two backends for storing alert instance state:\\n  - `store/instance_database.go` - Simple JSON-based instance storage\\n  - `store/proto_instance_database.go` - Protobuf-compressed instance storage (feature flag controlled)\\n\\nThe `DBstore` implements interfaces like `AlertingStore`, `RuleStore`, and `InstanceStore` that other components depend on.\\n\\n## 3. Scheduler (`schedule/`)\\n\\nThe scheduler is implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`. It contains:\\n\\n- **ScheduleService Interface**: Defines the scheduling contract\\n- **Rule Registry**: `schedule/registry.go` maintains loaded alert rules\\n- **Alert Rule Scheduling**: `schedule/alert_rule.go` handles alert rule evaluation scheduling\\n- **Recording Rule Scheduling**: `schedule/recording_rule.go` manages Prometheus recording rules\\n- **Rule Fetcher**: `schedule/fetcher.go` loads rules from the database\\n\\nThe scheduler uses a base interval tick system to evaluate rules at their configured intervals. It manages retry logic with exponential backoff for failed evaluations.\\n\\n## 4. State Manager (`state/`)\\n\\nThe state management subsystem is core to ngalert and implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`. Key components:\\n\\n- **Manager**: Central coordinator that tracks alert state in memory\\n- **State Transitions**: `state/state.go` defines state machines and transitions (normal, alerting, pending, no data)\\n- **State Cache**: `state/cache.go` holds in-memory alert state for fast access\\n- **State Persistence**: Multiple persister implementations:\\n  - `state/persister_sync.go` - Synchronous write to database\\n  - `state/persister_sync_rule.go` - Sync at rule group level\\n  - `state/persister_async.go` - Asynchronous batched writes\\n  - `state/persister_async_rule.go` - Async at rule group level\\n- **Instance Store Interface**: Multiple implementations for reading/writing instance state\\n  - `state/multi_instance_reader.go` - Reads from multiple backends during feature flag transitions\\n  - `state/store_state_reader.go` - Reads state from database (for HA mode)\\n\\n## 5. History Writer (`state/historian/` and `writer/`)\\n\\nThe history writer subsystem records all alert state transitions for audit trails and panel annotations. Implemented in:\\n\\n- **Historian Core**: `state/historian/core.go` - Logic for determining which transitions to record\\n  - `ShouldRecord()` - Decides if a transition should be written to history\\n  - `ShouldRecordAnnotation()` - Decides if dashboard annotations should be created\\n  - Label fingerprinting for stable alert identification\\n\\n- **Backend Abstraction**: `state/historian/backend.go` defines `BackendType`:\\n  - `annotations` - Stores in Grafana dashboard annotations\\n  - `loki` - Remote Loki for long-term retention\\n  - `prometheus` - Remote Prometheus for metrics\\n  - `multiple` - Hybrid multi-backend setup\\n  - `noop` - Disabled\\n\\n- **Backend Implementations**:\\n  - `state/historian/annotation.go` / `annotation_store.go` - Grafana annotations backend\\n  - `state/historian/loki.go` - Remote Loki backend\\n  - `state/historian/prometheus.go` - Remote Prometheus backend\\n  - `state/historian/multiple.go` - Multi-backend coordinator\\n\\n- **Remote Writer**: `writer/datasourcewriter.go` - Generic datasource writer for remote backends\\n\\n## 6. Notifier/Alertmanager (`notifier/`)\\n\\nThe notification subsystem manages alert routing and notification delivery:\\n\\n- **MultiOrgAlertmanager**: `notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go` - Multi-tenant wrapper\\n  - Manages per-organization Alertmanager instances\\n  - Handles configuration loading and synchronization\\n  - Manages clustering peers for HA deployments\\n  - Remote primary/secondary modes for delegated alertmanaging\\n\\n- **Alertmanager Interface**: `notifier/alertmanager.go` defines core operations:\\n  - Config management (apply, save, retrieve)\\n  - Silence operations (create, delete, list)\\n  - Alert operations (get, put)\\n  - Receiver management\\n  - Status tracking\\n\\n- **Configuration**: `notifier/alertmanager_config.go` - Alertmanager configuration handling\\n- **Auto-generation**: `notifier/autogen_alertmanager.go` - Default config generation\\n- **Receivers**: `notifier/receiver_svc.go` - Receiver CRUD operations\\n- **Silences**: `notifier/silence_svc.go` - Silence management\\n- **Sender**: `notifier/sender.go` - Alert sending to Alertmanager\\n\\n## 7. Alerts Router/Sender (`sender/`)\\n\\nResponsible for routing evaluated alerts to the Alertmanager:\\n\\n- **AlertsRouter**: `sender/router.go` - Main router that syncs config and routes alerts\\n  - Loads Alertmanager configuration from database\\n  - Applies configuration to Alertmanager instances\\n  - Periodically polls configuration for changes\\n  - Dispatches alerts to appropriate Alertmanager\\n\\n- **External Alertmanager Sender**: `sender/sender.go` - Sends alerts to external Alertmanagers\\n  - Queue-based alert batching\\n  - HTTP client management\\n  - Retry and backoff logic\\n\\n- **Notifier**: `sender/notifier.go` - Adapts alerts for Alertmanager format\\n\\n## 8. Evaluation (`eval/`)\\n\\nRule evaluation engine in `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/`:\\n\\n- **Evaluator**: `eval/eval.go` - Executes alert rule queries\\n  - Supports queries against Prometheus-compatible datasources\\n  - Supports Grafana expressions (math, reduce, etc.)\\n  - Returns numeric values with labels\\n  - Handles no-data and error conditions\\n\\n- **EvaluatorFactory**: Creates evaluators with proper dependencies\\n- **Validation**: `eval/validate.go` - Validates rule conditions before execution\\n- **Context**: `eval/context.go` - Execution context for evaluations\\n\\n## 9. Evaluation Runner\\n\\nThe `evaluationRunner` in `evaluation_runner.go` coordinates the evaluation pipeline:\\n\\n- Spawns goroutines for each rule evaluation\\n- Calls the scheduler to get rules\\n- Invokes evaluators\\n- Passes results to state manager\\n- Handles lifecycle (startup, shutdown)\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Startup**: `ngalert.go:init()` initializes all components, warming up state cache from database\\n2. **Scheduling**: Scheduler fetches rules from store and builds evaluation schedule\\n3. **Evaluation**: EvaluationRunner triggers rule evaluations at scheduled intervals\\n4. **State Management**: Evaluator results flow to State Manager which:\\n   - Compares against previous state\\n   - Generates StateTransition objects\\n   - Calls StatePersister to save state\\n   - Calls Historian to record changes\\n5. **Notification**: State transitions are sent to AlertsRouter which:\\n   - Formats alerts\\n   - Routes to Alertmanager\\n   - Alertmanager applies routing and sending rules\\n6. **Persistence**: History Writer backends persist state transitions for audit/dashboards\\n\\n## Key Interfaces\\n\\n- `AlertingStore` / `RuleStore` - Store layer contracts\\n- `ScheduleService` - Scheduler contract\\n- `AlertInstanceManager` - State access\\n- `Historian` - History writing\\n- `Alertmanager` - Notification interface\\n- `StatePersister` - State persistence\\n- `EvaluatorFactory` - Rule evaluation\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to evaluate alert rules at scale with support for HA deployments, multiple notification backends, and comprehensive state history tracking.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1470,"cache_read_input_tokens":74700,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1470},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"132e97cc-1217-4f00-9bd2-65c242aefbf4","uuid":"448dfef5-a078-4766-9d8b-f4357bb0f5e7"}

Grafana unified alerting subsystem is implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/` and consists of several interconnected major components:\\n\\n## 1. Service Orchestrator (`ngalert.go`)\\n\\nThe main entry point is `AlertNG` in `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`. The `ProvideService()` function initializes all components and `AlertNG.Run()` orchestrates their execution. The architecture follows a typical pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Alert Rule Storage** receives rules from the database\\n2. **Scheduler** fetches rules and determines evaluation timing\\n3. **Evaluator** executes rule queries against data sources\\n4. **State Manager** tracks alert state transitions\\n5. **History Writer** persists state changes for audit/dashboards\\n6. **Notifier** sends alerts through Alertmanager\\n7. **Alerts Router** dispatches to external Alertmanagers\\n\\n## 2. Alert Rule Storage (`store/`)\\n\\nThe storage layer is implemented by `DBstore` in `pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go`. This component manages:\\n\\n- **Alert Rules**: `store/alert_rule.go` - CRUD operations for alert rules\\n- **Alertmanager Config**: `store/alertmanager.go` - Configuration storage and versioning\\n- **Alert Instances**: Two backends for storing alert instance state:\\n  - `store/instance_database.go` - Simple JSON-based instance storage\\n  - `store/proto_instance_database.go` - Protobuf-compressed instance storage (feature flag controlled)\\n\\nThe `DBstore` implements interfaces like `AlertingStore`, `RuleStore`, and `InstanceStore` that other components depend on.\\n\\n## 3. Scheduler (`schedule/`)\\n\\nThe scheduler is implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`. It contains:\\n\\n- **ScheduleService Interface**: Defines the scheduling contract\\n- **Rule Registry**: `schedule/registry.go` maintains loaded alert rules\\n- **Alert Rule Scheduling**: `schedule/alert_rule.go` handles alert rule evaluation scheduling\\n- **Recording Rule Scheduling**: `schedule/recording_rule.go` manages Prometheus recording rules\\n- **Rule Fetcher**: `schedule/fetcher.go` loads rules from the database\\n\\nThe scheduler uses a base interval tick system to evaluate rules at their configured intervals. It manages retry logic with exponential backoff for failed evaluations.\\n\\n## 4. State Manager (`state/`)\\n\\nThe state management subsystem is core to ngalert and implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`. Key components:\\n\\n- **Manager**: Central coordinator that tracks alert state in memory\\n- **State Transitions**: `state/state.go` defines state machines and transitions (normal, alerting, pending, no data)\\n- **State Cache**: `state/cache.go` holds in-memory alert state for fast access\\n- **State Persistence**: Multiple persister implementations:\\n  - `state/persister_sync.go` - Synchronous write to database\\n  - `state/persister_sync_rule.go` - Sync at rule group level\\n  - `state/persister_async.go` - Asynchronous batched writes\\n  - `state/persister_async_rule.go` - Async at rule group level\\n- **Instance Store Interface**: Multiple implementations for reading/writing instance state\\n  - `state/multi_instance_reader.go` - Reads from multiple backends during feature flag transitions\\n  - `state/store_state_reader.go` - Reads state from database (for HA mode)\\n\\n## 5. History Writer (`state/historian/` and `writer/`)\\n\\nThe history writer subsystem records all alert state transitions for audit trails and panel annotations. Implemented in:\\n\\n- **Historian Core**: `state/historian/core.go` - Logic for determining which transitions to record\\n  - `ShouldRecord()` - Decides if a transition should be written to history\\n  - `ShouldRecordAnnotation()` - Decides if dashboard annotations should be created\\n  - Label fingerprinting for stable alert identification\\n\\n- **Backend Abstraction**: `state/historian/backend.go` defines `BackendType`:\\n  - `annotations` - Stores in Grafana dashboard annotations\\n  - `loki` - Remote Loki for long-term retention\\n  - `prometheus` - Remote Prometheus for metrics\\n  - `multiple` - Hybrid multi-backend setup\\n  - `noop` - Disabled\\n\\n- **Backend Implementations**:\\n  - `state/historian/annotation.go` / `annotation_store.go` - Grafana annotations backend\\n  - `state/historian/loki.go` - Remote Loki backend\\n  - `state/historian/prometheus.go` - Remote Prometheus backend\\n  - `state/historian/multiple.go` - Multi-backend coordinator\\n\\n- **Remote Writer**: `writer/datasourcewriter.go` - Generic datasource writer for remote backends\\n\\n## 6. Notifier/Alertmanager (`notifier/`)\\n\\nThe notification subsystem manages alert routing and notification delivery:\\n\\n- **MultiOrgAlertmanager**: `notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go` - Multi-tenant wrapper\\n  - Manages per-organization Alertmanager instances\\n  - Handles configuration loading and synchronization\\n  - Manages clustering peers for HA deployments\\n  - Remote primary/secondary modes for delegated alertmanaging\\n\\n- **Alertmanager Interface**: `notifier/alertmanager.go` defines core operations:\\n  - Config management (apply, save, retrieve)\\n  - Silence operations (create, delete, list)\\n  - Alert operations (get, put)\\n  - Receiver management\\n  - Status tracking\\n\\n- **Configuration**: `notifier/alertmanager_config.go` - Alertmanager configuration handling\\n- **Auto-generation**: `notifier/autogen_alertmanager.go` - Default config generation\\n- **Receivers**: `notifier/receiver_svc.go` - Receiver CRUD operations\\n- **Silences**: `notifier/silence_svc.go` - Silence management\\n- **Sender**: `notifier/sender.go` - Alert sending to Alertmanager\\n\\n## 7. Alerts Router/Sender (`sender/`)\\n\\nResponsible for routing evaluated alerts to the Alertmanager:\\n\\n- **AlertsRouter**: `sender/router.go` - Main router that syncs config and routes alerts\\n  - Loads Alertmanager configuration from database\\n  - Applies configuration to Alertmanager instances\\n  - Periodically polls configuration for changes\\n  - Dispatches alerts to appropriate Alertmanager\\n\\n- **External Alertmanager Sender**: `sender/sender.go` - Sends alerts to external Alertmanagers\\n  - Queue-based alert batching\\n  - HTTP client management\\n  - Retry and backoff logic\\n\\n- **Notifier**: `sender/notifier.go` - Adapts alerts for Alertmanager format\\n\\n## 8. Evaluation (`eval/`)\\n\\nRule evaluation engine in `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/`:\\n\\n- **Evaluator**: `eval/eval.go` - Executes alert rule queries\\n  - Supports queries against Prometheus-compatible datasources\\n  - Supports Grafana expressions (math, reduce, etc.)\\n  - Returns numeric values with labels\\n  - Handles no-data and error conditions\\n\\n- **EvaluatorFactory**: Creates evaluators with proper dependencies\\n- **Validation**: `eval/validate.go` - Validates rule conditions before execution\\n- **Context**: `eval/context.go` - Execution context for evaluations\\n\\n## 9. Evaluation Runner\\n\\nThe `evaluationRunner` in `evaluation_runner.go` coordinates the evaluation pipeline:\\n\\n- Spawns goroutines for each rule evaluation\\n- Calls the scheduler to get rules\\n- Invokes evaluators\\n- Passes results to state manager\\n- Handles lifecycle (startup, shutdown)\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Startup**: `ngalert.go:init()` initializes all components, warming up state cache from database\\n2. **Scheduling**: Scheduler fetches rules from store and builds evaluation schedule\\n3. **Evaluation**: EvaluationRunner triggers rule evaluations at scheduled intervals\\n4. **State Management**: Evaluator results flow to State Manager which:\\n   - Compares against previous state\\n   - Generates StateTransition objects\\n   - Calls StatePersister to save state\\n   - Calls Historian to record changes\\n5. **Notification**: State transitions are sent to AlertsRouter which:\\n   - Formats alerts\\n   - Routes to Alertmanager\\n   - Alertmanager applies routing and sending rules\\n6. **Persistence**: History Writer backends persist state transitions for audit/dashboards\\n\\n## Key Interfaces\\n\\n- `AlertingStore` / `RuleStore` - Store layer contracts\\n- `ScheduleService` - Scheduler contract\\n- `AlertInstanceManager` - State access\\n- `Historian` - History writing\\n- `Alertmanager` - Notification interface\\n- `StatePersister` - State persistence\\n- `EvaluatorFactory` - Rule evaluation\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to evaluate alert rules at scale with support for HA deployments, multiple notification backends, and comprehensive state history tracking.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
